select 'Sueroterapia' as Descripcion, 3 as id  
union  
select 'Laser' as Descripcion, 4 as id  
union 
select 'Intravenoso' as Descripcion, 5 as id  
union 
select 'Bloqueo' as Descripcion, 6 as id  
union 
select 'Celulas Madres' as Descripcion, 7 as id  
order by id
